@076B SDUG BSNGAL ZUG RNGU'I RTZA BA DRUNG NAS 'BYIN, ,RGYAL YUM
SHES RAB PHA ROL PHYIN LA SOGS, ,THEG GSUM DAM PA'I CHOS KYI
BKRA SHIS SHOG ,'JAM DBYANGS PHYAG NA RDO RJE SPYAN RAS GZIGS,
,SA YI SNYING PO SGRIB PA RNAM

PAR SEL, ,NAM MKHA'I SNYING PO BYAMS PA KUN TU BZANG, ,NYE BA'I
SRAS CHEN BRGYAD KYI BKRA SHIS SHOG ,ZAB MO RTEN 'BREL BCU GNYIS
LEGS BSGOMS PAS, ,RANG BYUNG RANG SANGS RGYAS KYI YE SHES NI,
,BSTEN PA

MED PA'I TSUL GYIS THUGS CHUD PA'I, ,'PHAGS PA RANG RGYAL RNAMS
KYI BKRA SHIS SHOG ,DUS GSUM RGYAL BA RGYAL SRAS THUGS RJE YIS,
,NYAN THOS TSUL BZUNG SRID PA JI SRID PAR, ,BSTAN PA SKYONG
ZHING 'GRO BA'I

DON MDZAD PA'I, ,GNAS BRTAN CHEN PO RNAMS KYI BKRA SHIS SHOG
,MKHA' LA SPYOD PA'I GNAS MCHOG DAM PA NAS, ,MNGON SHES RDZU
'PHRUL MNGA' BA'I MTHU STOBS CAN, ,SGRUB PA PO LA MA YIS BU
BZHIN GZIGS, ,

GNAS GSUM MKHA' 'GRO'I TSOGS KYI BKRA SHIS SHOG ,SNGON TSE BCOM
LDAN 'DAS KYI SPYAN SNGA RU, ,CHOS BZHIN SGRUB PA MDZAD PA'I
GANG ZAG LA, ,BU BZHIN SKYONG BAR ZHAL GYIS BZHES PA YI, ,CHOS
SKYONG SRUNG

MA'I TSOGS KYI BKRA SHIS SHOG ,LHUN GRUB CHOS DBYINGS PHO BRANG
DAM PA NAS, ,GDUGS PA 'DUL PHYIR DRAG MO'I SKU BSTAN YANG,
,DNGOS GRUB RIN CHEN 'DOD DGU'I CHAR 'BEBS MA, ,DMAG ZOR RGYAL
MO'I ZHABS KYI

@077A *, ,BKRA SHIS SHOG ,LEGS BSHAD RI MO BKRA BA'I LUNG GI
GOS, ,RNAM DPYOD GSER GYI YU BA LA BRTEN CING, ,BSLAB GSUM NOR
BU'I TOG GIS RAB MTSAN PA'I, ,BSTAN PA'I RGYAL MTSAN

PHYOGS BCUR TSUGS PAR SHOG ,SANGS RGYAS SKU GSUM BRNYES PA'I
BYIN RLABS DANG, ,CHOS NYID MI 'GYUR BDEN PA'I BYIN RLABS KYIS,
,JI LTAR BSNGO BA SMON LAM 'GRUB PAR SHOG , ,,

@077B ` RNAM GROL ZHI BA'I RGYA MTSO RO GCIG TU, ,GZHOL BA'I
MTHA' YAS CHOS TSUL DAL BAB KLUNG,,

TSIG GI GZEGS MA RES KYANG DUG GSUM GYI, ,DRI MA YONGS 'KHRUD
LEGS BSHAD BDUD RTZI 'DI, ,DPAR DU BSKRUN PA'I RNAM DKAR PHUNG
PO'I MTHUS, ,YANG DAG CHOS KYI SGO MA STONG PHRAG BRGYA, ,GDANGS
TE RGYUD

LNGA'I 'GRO BA MA LUS PA, ,NGES LEGS NOR BU'I MDZOD LA DBANG
'BYOR SHOG , ,,{ CES DGE BSNGO'I SMON TSIG 'DI BZHIN 'DZAM GLING
GZHI BDE'I DED DPON CHEN PO ^GONG SA LHA MI'I RNAMS 'DREN CHEN
PO SKYABS MGON ^RGYAL DBANG

THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA SKU PHRENG BCU BZHI PA CHEN POS MDZAD PA'O
